### File 10: gradlew
**Path:** `android\gradlew`
**Size:** 4.85 KB

```text
#!/usr/bin/env bash

##############################################################################
##
##  Gradle start up script for UN*X
##
##############################################################################

# Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=""

APP_NAME="Gradle"
APP_BASE_NAME=`basename "$0"`

# Use the maximum available, or set MAX_FD != -1 to use that value.
MAX_FD="maximum"

warn ( ) {
    echo "$*"
}

die ( ) {
    echo
    echo "$*"
    echo
    exit 1
}

# OS specific support (must be 'true' or 'false').
cygwin=false
msys=false
darwin=false
case "`uname`" in
  CYGWIN* )
    cygwin=true
    ;;
  Darwin* )
    darwin=true
    ;;
  MINGW* )
    msys=true
    ;;
esac

# Attempt to set APP_HOME
# Resolve links: $0 may be a link
PRG="$0"
# Need this for relative symlinks.
while [ -h "$PRG" ] ; do
    ls=`ls -ld "$PRG"`
    link=`expr "$ls" : '.*-> \(.*\)$'`
    if expr "$link" : '/.*' > /dev/null; then
        PRG="$link"
    else
        PRG=`dirname "$PRG"`"/$link"
    fi
done
SAVED="`pwd`"
cd "`dirname \"$PRG\"`/" >/dev/null
APP_HOME="`pwd -P`"
cd "$SAVED" >/dev/null

CLASSPATH=$APP_HOME/gradle/wrapper/gradle-wrapper.jar

# Determine the Java command to use to start the JVM.
if [ -n "$JAVA_HOME" ] ; then
    if [ -x "$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java" ] ; then
        # IBM's JDK on AIX uses strange locations for the executables
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java"
    else
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/bin/java"
    fi
    if [ ! -x "$JAVACMD" ] ; then
        die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: $JAVA_HOME

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
    fi
else
    JAVACMD="java"
    which java >/dev/null 2>&1 || die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
fi

# Increase the maximum file descriptors if we can.
if [ "$cygwin" = "false" -a "$darwin" = "false" ] ; then
    MAX_FD_LIMIT=`ulimit -H -n`
    if [ $? -eq 0 ] ; then
        if [ "$MAX_FD" = "maximum" -o "$MAX_FD" = "max" ] ; then
            MAX_FD="$MAX_FD_LIMIT"
        fi
        ulimit -n $MAX_FD
        if [ $? -ne 0 ] ; then
            warn "Could not set maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD"
        fi
    else
        warn "Could not query maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD_LIMIT"
    fi
fi

# For Darwin, add options to specify how the application appears in the dock
if $darwin; then
    GRADLE_OPTS="$GRADLE_OPTS \"-Xdock:name=$APP_NAME\" \"-Xdock:icon=$APP_HOME/media/gradle.icns\""
fi

# For Cygwin, switch paths to Windows format before running java
if $cygwin ; then
    APP_HOME=`cygpath --path --mixed "$APP_HOME"`
    CLASSPATH=`cygpath --path --mixed "$CLASSPATH"`
    JAVACMD=`cygpath --unix "$JAVACMD"`

    # We build the pattern for arguments to be converted via cygpath
    ROOTDIRSRAW=`find -L / -maxdepth 1 -mindepth 1 -type d 2>/dev/null`
    SEP=""
    for dir in $ROOTDIRSRAW ; do
        ROOTDIRS="$ROOTDIRS$SEP$dir"
        SEP="|"
    done
    OURCYGPATTERN="(^($ROOTDIRS))"
    # Add a user-defined pattern to the cygpath arguments
    if [ "$GRADLE_CYGPATTERN" != "" ] ; then
        OURCYGPATTERN="$OURCYGPATTERN|($GRADLE_CYGPATTERN)"
    fi
    # Now convert the arguments - kludge to limit ourselves to /bin/sh
    i=0
    for arg in "$@" ; do
        CHECK=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "$OURCYGPATTERN" -`
        CHECK2=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "^-"`                                 ### Determine if an option

        if [ $CHECK -ne 0 ] && [ $CHECK2 -eq 0 ] ; then                    ### Added a condition
            eval `echo args$i`=`cygpath --path --ignore --mixed "$arg"`
        else
            eval `echo args$i`="\"$arg\""
        fi
        i=$((i+1))
    done
    case $i in
        (0) set -- ;;
        (1) set -- "$args0" ;;
        (2) set -- "$args0" "$args1" ;;
        (3) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" ;;
        (4) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" ;;
        (5) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" ;;
        (6) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" ;;
        (7) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" ;;
        (8) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" ;;
        (9) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" "$args8" ;;
    esac
fi

# Split up the JVM_OPTS And GRADLE_OPTS values into an array, following the shell quoting and substitution rules
function splitJvmOpts() {
    JVM_OPTS=("$@")
}
eval splitJvmOpts $DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS $JAVA_OPTS $GRADLE_OPTS
JVM_OPTS[${#JVM_OPTS[*]}]="-Dorg.gradle.appname=$APP_BASE_NAME"

exec "$JAVACMD" "${JVM_OPTS[@]}" -classpath "$CLASSPATH" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain "$@"

```

### File 11: gradlew.bat
**Path:** `android\gradlew.bat`
**Size:** 2.35 KB

```text
@if "%DEBUG%" == "" @echo off
@rem ##########################################################################
@rem
@rem  Gradle startup script for Windows
@rem
@rem ##########################################################################

@rem Set local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" setlocal

@rem Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
set DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=

set DIRNAME=%~dp0
if "%DIRNAME%" == "" set DIRNAME=.
set APP_BASE_NAME=%~n0
set APP_HOME=%DIRNAME%

@rem Find java.exe
if defined JAVA_HOME goto findJavaFromJavaHome

set JAVA_EXE=java.exe
%JAVA_EXE% -version >NUL 2>&1
if "%ERRORLEVEL%" == "0" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:findJavaFromJavaHome
set JAVA_HOME=%JAVA_HOME:"=%
set JAVA_EXE=%JAVA_HOME%/bin/java.exe

if exist "%JAVA_EXE%" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: %JAVA_HOME%
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:init
@rem Get command-line arguments, handling Windowz variants

if not "%OS%" == "Windows_NT" goto win9xME_args
if "%@eval[2+2]" == "4" goto 4NT_args

:win9xME_args
@rem Slurp the command line arguments.
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=
set _SKIP=2

:win9xME_args_slurp
if "x%~1" == "x" goto execute

set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%*
goto execute

:4NT_args
@rem Get arguments from the 4NT Shell from JP Software
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%$

:execute
@rem Setup the command line

set CLASSPATH=%APP_HOME%\gradle\wrapper\gradle-wrapper.jar

@rem Execute Gradle
"%JAVA_EXE%" %DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS% %JAVA_OPTS% %GRADLE_OPTS% "-Dorg.gradle.appname=%APP_BASE_NAME%" -classpath "%CLASSPATH%" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain %CMD_LINE_ARGS%

:end
@rem End local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%ERRORLEVEL%"=="0" goto mainEnd

:fail
rem Set variable GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE if you need the _script_ return code instead of
rem the _cmd.exe /c_ return code!
if  not "" == "%GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE%" exit 1
exit /b 1

:mainEnd
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" endlocal

:omega

```

### File 15: GeneratedPluginRegistrant.java

```java
package io.flutter.plugins;

import androidx.annotation.Keep;
import androidx.annotation.NonNull;
import io.flutter.Log;

import io.flutter.embedding.engine.FlutterEngine;

/**
 * Generated file. Do not edit.
 * This file is generated by the Flutter tool based on the
 * plugins that support the Android platform.
 */
@Keep
public final class GeneratedPluginRegistrant {
  private static final String TAG = "GeneratedPluginRegistrant";
  public static void registerWith(@NonNull FlutterEngine flutterEngine) {
    try {
      flutterEngine.getPlugins().add(new io.flutter.plugins.pathprovider.PathProviderPlugin());
    } catch (Exception e) {
      Log.e(TAG, "Error registering plugin path_provider_android, io.flutter.plugins.pathprovider.PathProviderPlugin", e);
    }
    try {
      flutterEngine.getPlugins().add(new dev.fluttercommunity.plus.share.SharePlusPlugin());
    } catch (Exception e) {
      Log.e(TAG, "Error registering plugin share_plus, dev.fluttercommunity.plus.share.SharePlusPlugin", e);
    }
    try {
      flutterEngine.getPlugins().add(new io.flutter.plugins.sharedpreferences.SharedPreferencesPlugin());
    } catch (Exception e) {
      Log.e(TAG, "Error registering plugin shared_preferences_android, io.flutter.plugins.sharedpreferences.SharedPreferencesPlugin", e);
    }
    try {
      flutterEngine.getPlugins().add(new com.jaumard.smsautofill.SmsAutoFillPlugin());
    } catch (Exception e) {
      Log.e(TAG, "Error registering plugin sms_autofill, com.jaumard.smsautofill.SmsAutoFillPlugin", e);
    }
  }
}
```

```kotlin
package com.prahlad.emipro.emi_pro

import io.flutter.embedding.android.FlutterActivity

class MainActivity: FlutterActivity() {
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        // Let Flutter handle back navigation
        val engine = flutterEngine
        if (engine != null) {
            engine.navigationChannel.popRoute()
        } else {
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }
}

```

### File 22: gradle-wrapper.properties

```text
distributionBase=GRADLE_USER_HOME
distributionPath=wrapper/dists
```

### File 29: main.dart
**Path:** `lib\main.dart`
**Size:** 2.04 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import 'screens/splash_screen.dart';
import 'screens/login_screen.dart';
import 'screens/home_dashboard_screen.dart';

void main() {
  runApp(const EMIProApp());
}

class EMIProApp extends StatelessWidget {
  const EMIProApp({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      title: 'EMI Pro',
      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
      theme: ThemeData(
        primaryColor: const Color(0xFF1E88E5),
        fontFamily: 'Inter',
        useMaterial3: true,
      ),
      home: const AuthChecker(),
    );
  }
}

class AuthChecker extends StatefulWidget {
  const AuthChecker({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  State<AuthChecker> createState() => _AuthCheckerState();
}

class _AuthCheckerState extends State<AuthChecker> {
  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _checkLoginStatus();
  }

  Future<void> _checkLoginStatus() async {
    await Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 2));

    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final isLoggedIn = prefs.getBool('is_logged_in') ?? false;
    final loginTimestamp = prefs.getInt('login_timestamp') ?? 0;

    final currentTime = DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch;
    final isLoginValid = (currentTime - loginTimestamp) < 86400000; // 24 hours

    if (!mounted) return;

    if (isLoggedIn && isLoginValid) {
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const HomeDashboardScreen()),
      );
    } else {
      if (!isLoginValid && isLoggedIn) {
        await prefs.setBool('is_logged_in', false);
        await prefs.remove('login_timestamp');
      }
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const LoginScreen()),
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return const SplashScreen();
  }
}

```

### File 30: saved_calculation_model.dart
**Path:** `lib\models\saved_calculation_model.dart`
**Size:** 1.52 KB

```dart
import 'dart:convert';

class SavedCalculationModel {
  final String id;
  final String type; // 'Home Loan', 'Car Loan', etc.
  final double principalAmount;
  final double interestRate;
  final double tenure; // Always stored in YEARS (whole number)
  final double monthlyEMI;
  final DateTime date;

  SavedCalculationModel({
    required this.id,
    required this.type,
    required this.principalAmount,
    required this.interestRate,
    required this.tenure,
    required this.monthlyEMI,
    required this.date,
  });

  Map<String, dynamic> toMap() {
    return {
      'id': id,
      'type': type,
      'principalAmount': principalAmount,
      // Fix: Store raw values for better precision when editing later
      'interestRate': interestRate,
      'tenure': tenure,
      'monthlyEMI': monthlyEMI,
      'date': date.toIso8601String(),
    };
  }

  factory SavedCalculationModel.fromMap(Map<String, dynamic> map) {
    return SavedCalculationModel(
      id: map['id'],
      type: map['type'],
      // Fix: Ensure double parsing is safe
      principalAmount: (map['principalAmount'] as num).toDouble(),
      interestRate: (map['interestRate'] as num).toDouble(),
      tenure: (map['tenure'] as num).toDouble(),
      monthlyEMI: (map['monthlyEMI'] as num).toDouble(),
      date: DateTime.parse(map['date']),
    );
  }

  String toJson() => json.encode(toMap());

  factory SavedCalculationModel.fromJson(String source) =>
      SavedCalculationModel.fromMap(json.decode(source));
}
```

### File 31: car_loan_calculator_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\car_loan_calculator_screen.dart`
**Size:** 3.52 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../utils/car_loan_colors.dart';
import '../../services/loan_calculator_helpers.dart';
// Widget Imports
import '../widgets/car_loan/car_loan_app_bar.dart';
import '../widgets/car_loan/car_loan_result_card.dart';
import '../widgets/car_loan/car_loan_input_card.dart';
import '../widgets/car_loan/car_loan_breakdown_card.dart';
import '../widgets/car_loan/car_loan_bottom_bar.dart';

class CarLoanCalculatorScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const CarLoanCalculatorScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<CarLoanCalculatorScreen> createState() => _CarLoanState();
}

class _CarLoanState extends State<CarLoanCalculatorScreen> {
  // Default Values for Car Loan
  double _amount = 800000;
  double _rate = 9.5;
  double _tenure = 5; // Default 5 Years
  bool _isYears = true;

  // Results
  double _emi = 0, _interest = 0, _total = 0;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _calculate();
  }

  void _calculate() {
    // Logic: Always convert to months for calculation
    double months = _isYears ? _tenure * 12 : _tenure;
    if (months <= 0) months = 1;

    double emi = LoanCalculatorHelpers.calculateEMI(_amount, _rate, months);

    setState(() {
      _emi = emi;
      _total = emi * months;
      _interest = _total - _amount;
    });
  }

  // Toggle between Years and Months correctly
  void _toggleType(bool isYears) {
    setState(() {
      if (_isYears && !isYears) {
        // Was Years, Now Months (e.g., 5 yrs -> 60 months)
        _tenure = (_tenure * 12).clamp(1, 120);
      } else if (!_isYears && isYears) {
        // Was Months, Now Years (e.g., 60 months -> 5 yrs)
        _tenure = (_tenure / 12).clamp(1, 10);
      }
      _isYears = isYears;
      _calculate();
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: CarLoanColors.background,
      body: Column(
        children: [
          CarLoanAppBar(
            onBack: () => Navigator.pop(context),
            onBookmark: () => ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                const SnackBar(content: Text("Bookmark feature coming soon!"))
            ),
          ),
          Expanded(
            child: SingleChildScrollView(
              child: Column(
                children: [
                  const SizedBox(height: 16),
                  CarLoanResultCard(emi: _emi, interestRate: _rate, tenure: _tenure, isYears: _isYears),
                  CarLoanInputCard(
                    amount: _amount, rate: _rate, tenure: _tenure, isYears: _isYears,
                    onAmountChanged: (v) { setState(() => _amount = v); _calculate(); },
                    onRateChanged: (v) { setState(() => _rate = v); _calculate(); },
                    onTenureChanged: (v) { setState(() => _tenure = v); _calculate(); },
                    onTypeChanged: _toggleType,
                  ),
                  CarLoanBreakdownCard(principal: _amount, interest: _interest, total: _total),
                ],
              ),
            ),
          ),
          CarLoanBottomBar(
            onAmortization: () {
              ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(const SnackBar(content: Text("Amortization Table Coming Soon")));
            },
            onSave: () {
              ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text("Calculation Saved: â‚¹${_emi.toStringAsFixed(0)}/mo")));
            },
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 33: history_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\history_screen.dart`
**Size:** 3.26 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import '../models/saved_calculation_model.dart';
import '../utils/app_colors.dart';
import '../widgets/history/saved_calculation_card.dart';

class HistoryScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const HistoryScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<HistoryScreen> createState() => _HistoryScreenState();
}

class _HistoryScreenState extends State<HistoryScreen> {
  List<SavedCalculationModel> _calculations = [];
  bool _isLoading = true;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _loadHistory();
  }

  Future<void> _loadHistory() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final List<String>? historyJson = prefs.getStringList('calculations');

    if (historyJson != null) {
      setState(() {
        _calculations = historyJson
            .map((item) => SavedCalculationModel.fromJson(item))
            .toList()
            .reversed // Show newest first
            .toList();
      });
    }
    setState(() => _isLoading = false);
  }

  Future<void> _deleteCalculation(String id) async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    setState(() {
      _calculations.removeWhere((item) => item.id == id);
    });

    // Update local storage
    final List<String> updatedList = _calculations
        .map((item) => item.toJson())
        .toList()
        .reversed // Reverse back for storage
        .toList();

    await prefs.setStringList('calculations', updatedList);

    if (mounted) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        const SnackBar(content: Text('Calculation deleted')),
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundLight,
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: const Text('Saved Calculations', style: TextStyle(color: Colors.black)),
        backgroundColor: Colors.white,
        elevation: 0,
        actions: [
          IconButton(
            icon: const Icon(Icons.share, color: AppColors.primaryBlue),
            onPressed: () {
              // Export logic can go here
              ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                const SnackBar(content: Text('Export All feature coming soon')),
              );
            },
          )
        ],
      ),
      body: _isLoading
          ? const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator())
          : _calculations.isEmpty
          ? Center(
        child: Column(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: [
            Icon(Icons.history, size: 64, color: Colors.grey[300]),
            const SizedBox(height: 16),
            Text('No history yet',
                style: TextStyle(color: Colors.grey[600], fontSize: 16)),
          ],
        ),
      )
          : ListView.builder(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
        itemCount: _calculations.length,
        itemBuilder: (context, index) {
          final calc = _calculations[index];
          return SavedCalculationCard(
            data: calc,
            onDelete: () => _deleteCalculation(calc.id),
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 35: home_loan_calculator_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\home_loan_calculator_screen.dart`
**Size:** 6.56 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../utils/app_colors.dart';
import '../../services/loan_calculator_helpers.dart';
import '../../widgets/calculator/loan_calculator_app_bar.dart';
import '../../widgets/calculator/loan_calculator_inputs.dart';
import '../../widgets/calculator/loan_calculator_result_card.dart';
import '../../widgets/calculator/loan_calculator_breakdown.dart';
import '../../widgets/calculator/loan_calculator_bottom_actions.dart';
import '../../widgets/calculator/loan_calculator_pie_chart.dart';
import 'home_dashboard_screen.dart';

class HomeLoanCalculatorScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const HomeLoanCalculatorScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<HomeLoanCalculatorScreen> createState() => _HomeLoanCalculatorScreenState();
}

class _HomeLoanCalculatorScreenState extends State<HomeLoanCalculatorScreen> {
  // Initial Values
  double _loanAmount = 2500000;
  double _interestRate = 8.5;
  double _loanTenure = 20; // Default in Years
  bool _isYears = true;

  // Results
  double _monthlyEMI = 0;
  double _totalInterest = 0;
  double _totalAmount = 0;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _calculateEMI();
  }

  void _calculateEMI() {
    // Logic: Always convert to months for calculation
    double tenureInMonths = _isYears ? _loanTenure * 12 : _loanTenure;

    // Prevent division by zero or negative tenure
    if (tenureInMonths <= 0) tenureInMonths = 1;

    double emi = LoanCalculatorHelpers.calculateEMI(_loanAmount, _interestRate, tenureInMonths);

    // Safety check for NaN or Infinite
    if (emi.isNaN || emi.isInfinite) emi = 0;

    double totalPayable = emi * tenureInMonths;
    double totalInterest = totalPayable - _loanAmount;

    // Handle case where interest is 0 or negative results
    if (totalInterest < 0) totalInterest = 0;

    setState(() {
      _monthlyEMI = emi;
      _totalAmount = totalPayable;
      _totalInterest = totalInterest;
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundLight,
      body: SafeArea(
        child: Column(
          children: [
            LoanCalculatorAppBar(
              onBackPressed: () {
                if (Navigator.canPop(context)) {
                  Navigator.pop(context);
                } else {
                  Navigator.pushReplacement(
                    context,
                    MaterialPageRoute(
                      builder: (context) => const HomeDashboardScreen(),
                    ),
                  );
                }
              },
              onBookmarkPressed: () {
                ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                  const SnackBar(content: Text('Bookmark feature coming soon')),
                );
              },
            ),

            Expanded(
              child: SingleChildScrollView(
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    LoanCalculatorInputs(
                      loanAmount: _loanAmount,
                      interestRate: _interestRate,
                      tenure: _loanTenure,
                      isYears: _isYears,
                      onLoanAmountChanged: (val) {
                        setState(() => _loanAmount = val);
                        _calculateEMI();
                      },
                      onInterestRateChanged: (val) {
                        setState(() => _interestRate = val);
                        _calculateEMI();
                      },
                      onTenureChanged: (val) {
                        setState(() => _loanTenure = val);
                        _calculateEMI();
                      },
                      onTenureTypeChanged: (bool isNowYears) {
                        setState(() {
                          // Logic: Convert value correctly when switching
                          if (_isYears && !isNowYears) {
                            // Was Years, Now Months -> Multiply by 12
                            _loanTenure = _loanTenure * 12;
                            // Clamp to reasonable max months (e.g., 30 years * 12 = 360)
                            if (_loanTenure > 360) _loanTenure = 360;
                          } else if (!_isYears && isNowYears) {
                            // Was Months, Now Years -> Divide by 12
                            _loanTenure = _loanTenure / 12;
                            // Clamp to reasonable max years
                            if (_loanTenure > 30) _loanTenure = 30;
                          }
                          _isYears = isNowYears;
                        });
                        _calculateEMI();
                      },
                    ),

                    const SizedBox(height: 16),

                    Padding(
                      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
                      child: LoanCalculatorResultCard(
                        monthlyEMI: _monthlyEMI,
                        tenure: _loanTenure,
                        interestRate: _interestRate,
                        isYears: _isYears,
                      ),
                    ),

                    const SizedBox(height: 16),

                    Padding(
                      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
                      child: LoanCalculatorBreakdown(
                        loanAmount: _loanAmount,
                        totalInterest: _totalInterest,
                        totalAmount: _totalAmount,
                      ),
                    ),

                    const SizedBox(height: 16),

                    Padding(
                      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
                      child: LoanCalculatorPieChart(
                        loanAmount: _loanAmount,
                        totalInterest: _totalInterest,
                        totalAmount: _totalAmount,
                      ),
                    ),

                    const SizedBox(height: 100), // Space for bottom sheet
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      bottomSheet: LoanCalculatorBottomActions(
        loanAmount: _loanAmount,
        monthlyEMI: _monthlyEMI,
        interestRate: _interestRate,
        totalInterest: _totalInterest,
        tenure: _loanTenure,
        isYears: _isYears,
        tenureInMonths: _isYears ? _loanTenure * 12 : _loanTenure,
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import '../widgets/login/login_header.dart';
import '../widgets/login/login_form.dart';
import '../widgets/login/login_validator.dart';
import '../widgets/login/login_footer.dart';
import 'signup_screen.dart';
import 'home_dashboard_screen.dart';

class LoginScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const LoginScreen({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  State<LoginScreen> createState() => _LoginScreenState();
}

class _LoginScreenState extends State<LoginScreen> {
  final _phoneController = TextEditingController();
  final _passwordController = TextEditingController();

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _phoneController.dispose();
    _passwordController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  Future<void> _handleLogin() async {
    final validator = LoginValidator(context);

    final success = await validator.validateAndLogin(
      phone: _phoneController.text,
      password: _passwordController.text,
    );

    if (success && mounted) {
      // Save login status with timestamp
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
      await prefs.setBool('is_logged_in', true);
      await prefs.setInt('login_timestamp', DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch);
      await prefs.setString('user_phone', _phoneController.text);

      // Save user name
      final userName = _phoneController.text.startsWith('93254')
          ? 'Prahlad Das'
          : 'User';
      await prefs.setString('user_name', userName);

      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const HomeDashboardScreen()),
      );
    }
  }

  void _handleSkip() async {
    // Save guest login status
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.setBool('is_logged_in', true);
    await prefs.setInt('login_timestamp', DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch);
    await prefs.setString('user_name', 'Guest User');

    if (!mounted) return;

    Navigator.pushReplacement(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const HomeDashboardScreen()),
    );
  }

  void _navigateToSignup() {
    Navigator.push(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const SignupScreen()),
    );
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: SingleChildScrollView(
        child: Column(
          children: [
            const LoginHeader(),
            Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24.0),
              child: Transform.translate(
                offset: const Offset(0, -60),
                child: Card(
                  elevation: 8,
                  shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
                    borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
                  ),
                  child: Padding(
                    padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
                    child: Column(
                      children: [
                        LoginForm(
                          phoneController: _phoneController,
                          passwordController: _passwordController,
                          onLogin: _handleLogin,
                        ),
                        LoginFooter(
                          onSignupTap: _navigateToSignup,
                          onSkipTap: _handleSkip,
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'dart:developer' as developer;
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:sms_autofill/sms_autofill.dart';
import '../utils/app_colors.dart';
import '../widgets/otp/otp_header.dart';
import '../widgets/otp/otp_generator.dart';
import '../widgets/otp/otp_input_widget.dart';
import 'home_dashboard_screen.dart';

class OtpVerificationScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String phoneNumber;

  const OtpVerificationScreen({
    Key? key,
    required this.phoneNumber,
  }) : super(key: key);

  @override
  State<OtpVerificationScreen> createState() => _OtpVerificationScreenState();
}

class _OtpVerificationScreenState extends State<OtpVerificationScreen> with CodeAutoFill {
  final List<TextEditingController> _otpControllers = List.generate(
    6,
        (index) => TextEditingController(),
  );
  late OtpGenerator _otpGenerator;

  int _secondsRemaining = 45;
  bool _canResend = false;
  String? appSignature;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _otpGenerator = OtpGenerator();
    _startTimer();
    _initializeSmsListener();
    _showOtpInConsole();
    _sendSmsNotification();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    cancel();
    for (var controller in _otpControllers) {
      controller.dispose();
    }
    super.dispose();
  }

  void _initializeSmsListener() async {
    appSignature = await SmsAutoFill().getAppSignature;
    developer.log('App Signature: $appSignature', name: 'SMS Auto-fill');
    listenForCode();
  }

  @override
  void codeUpdated() {
    if (code != null && code!.length == 6) {
      setState(() {
        for (int i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
          _otpControllers[i].text = code![i];
        }
      });

      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        const SnackBar(
          content: Row(
            children: [
              Icon(Icons.done_all, color: Colors.white, size: 20),
              SizedBox(width: 12),
              Text('OTP auto-filled from SMS!'),
            ],
          ),
          backgroundColor: Colors.blue,
          duration: Duration(seconds: 2),
          behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  void _showOtpInConsole() {
    developer.log('ğŸ” Generated OTP: ${_otpGenerator.generatedOtp}', name: 'EMI Pro');
    print('\nâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•');
    print('ğŸ“± EMI Pro - OTP Verification');
    print('ğŸ“ To: ${widget.phoneNumber}');
    print('ğŸ” YOUR OTP IS: ${_otpGenerator.generatedOtp}');
    print('ğŸ”‘ App Signature: $appSignature');
    print('â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n');

    final smsFormat = '<#> EMI Pro: Your OTP for phone verification is ${_otpGenerator.generatedOtp}. Valid for 5 minutes. $appSignature';
    print('ğŸ“© SMS FORMAT (for real SMS service):');
    print(smsFormat);
    print('');
  }

  void _sendSmsNotification() {
    WidgetsBinding.instance.addPostFrameCallback((_) {
      if (mounted) {
        final smsMessage = 'EMI Pro: Your OTP for phone verification is ${_otpGenerator.generatedOtp}. Valid for 5 minutes. Do not share with anyone.';

        print('ğŸ“© SMS SENT:');
        print('From: EMI-PRO');
        print('Message: $smsMessage\n');

        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Column(
              mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                const Row(
                  children: [
                    Icon(Icons.message, color: Colors.white, size: 16),
                    SizedBox(width: 8),
                    Text(
                      'EMI Pro',
                      style: TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, fontSize: 14),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 6),
                Text(
                  'Your OTP: ${_otpGenerator.generatedOtp}',
                  style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 16, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 4),
                const Text(
                  'Auto-filling OTP...',
                  style: TextStyle(fontSize: 11, color: Colors.white70),
                ),
              ],
            ),
            backgroundColor: Colors.green,
            duration: const Duration(seconds: 5),
            behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
          ),
        );

        // Auto-fill simulation after 1.5 seconds
        Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 1500), () {
          if (mounted) {
            String otp = _otpGenerator.generatedOtp;
            setState(() {
              for (int i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
                _otpControllers[i].text = otp[i];
              }
            });

            ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
              const SnackBar(
                content: Row(
                  children: [
                    Icon(Icons.done_all, color: Colors.white, size: 20),
                    SizedBox(width: 12),
                    Text('OTP auto-filled successfully!'),
                  ],
                ),
                backgroundColor: Colors.blue,
                duration: Duration(seconds: 2),
                behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
              ),
            );
          }
        });
      }
    });
  }

  void _startTimer() {
    Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 1), () {
      if (mounted && _secondsRemaining > 0) {
        setState(() => _secondsRemaining--);
        _startTimer();
      } else if (mounted) {
        setState(() => _canResend = true);
      }
    });
  }

  void _resetTimer() {
    setState(() {
      _secondsRemaining = 45;
      _canResend = false;
    });
    _startTimer();
  }

  void _verifyOtp() {
    String enteredOtp = _otpControllers.map((c) => c.text).join();

    if (enteredOtp.length != 6) {
      _showError('Please enter complete 6-digit OTP');
      return;
    }

    if (_otpGenerator.verifyOtp(enteredOtp)) {
      _showSuccess('âœ“ OTP Verified Successfully!');
      Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 1), () {
        if (mounted) {
          Navigator.pushReplacement(
            context,
            MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const HomeDashboardScreen()),
          );
        }
      });
    } else {
      _showError('Invalid OTP. Please try again');
      for (var controller in _otpControllers) {
        controller.clear();
      }
    }
  }

  void _resendOtp() {
    for (var controller in _otpControllers) {
      controller.clear();
    }
    _otpGenerator.generateNewOtp();
    _resetTimer();
    _showOtpInConsole();
    _sendSmsNotification();
    listenForCode();

    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      const SnackBar(
        content: Row(
          children: [
            Icon(Icons.refresh, color: Colors.white, size: 20),
            SizedBox(width: 12),
            Text('New OTP sent!'),
          ],
        ),
        backgroundColor: Colors.blue,
        duration: Duration(seconds: 2),
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showError(String message) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Row(
          children: [
            const Icon(Icons.error_outline, color: Colors.white),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),
            Expanded(child: Text(message)),
          ],
        ),
        backgroundColor: Colors.red,
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showSuccess(String message) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Row(
          children: [
            const Icon(Icons.check_circle, color: Colors.white),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),
            Text(message),
          ],
        ),
        backgroundColor: Colors.green,
        behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
      ),
    );
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(
        decoration: BoxDecoration(gradient: AppColors.primaryGradient),
        child: SafeArea(
          child: Column(
            children: [
              OtpHeader(
                phoneNumber: widget.phoneNumber,
                onBack: () => Navigator.pop(context),
                onEditNumber: () => Navigator.pop(context),
              ),
              Expanded(
                child: SingleChildScrollView(
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
                  child: Card(
                    elevation: 8,
                    shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
                      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
                    ),
                    child: Padding(
                      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
                      child: Column(
                        children: [
                          OtpInputWidget(controllers: _otpControllers),
                          const SizedBox(height: 24),
                          _buildTimerSection(),
                          const SizedBox(height: 32),
                          _buildVerifyButton(),
                          const SizedBox(height: 16),
                          _buildSupportLink(),
                        ],
                      ),
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildTimerSection() {
    String minutes = (_secondsRemaining ~/ 60).toString().padLeft(2, '0');
    String seconds = (_secondsRemaining % 60).toString().padLeft(2, '0');

    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
      children: [
        const Icon(Icons.schedule, color: Colors.grey, size: 18),
        const SizedBox(width: 8),
        if (!_canResend)
          Text('Resend code in $minutes:$seconds',
              style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.grey))
        else
          TextButton(
            onPressed: _resendOtp,
            child: const Text('Resend Code'),
          ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildVerifyButton() {
    return SizedBox(
      width: double.infinity,
      child: ElevatedButton(
        onPressed: _verifyOtp,
        style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
          backgroundColor: AppColors.primaryBlue,
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
          shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12)),
        ),
        child: const Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: [
            Text('Verify & Continue',
                style: TextStyle(fontSize: 16, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold)),
            SizedBox(width: 8),
            Icon(Icons.arrow_forward, size: 20),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildSupportLink() {
    return const Text.rich(
      TextSpan(
        text: 'Having trouble? ',
        style: TextStyle(color: Colors.grey),
        children: [
          TextSpan(
            text: 'Contact Support',
            style: TextStyle(
              color: AppColors.primaryBlue,
              decoration: TextDecoration.underline,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 38: personal_loan_calculator_screen.dart

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../services/loan_calculator_helpers.dart';
import '../../utils/personal_loan_colors.dart';
import '../widgets/personal_loan/personal_loan_app_bar.dart';
import '../widgets/personal_loan/personal_loan_result_card.dart';
import '../widgets/personal_loan/personal_loan_input_card.dart';
import '../widgets/personal_loan/personal_loan_breakdown_card.dart';
import '../widgets/personal_loan/personal_loan_bottom_bar.dart';

class PersonalLoanCalculatorScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const PersonalLoanCalculatorScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<PersonalLoanCalculatorScreen> createState() => _PersonalLoanState();
}

class _PersonalLoanState extends State<PersonalLoanCalculatorScreen> {
  // HTML Defaults: 2L Amount, 12% Rate, 3 Years
  double _amount = 200000;
  double _rate = 12.0;
  double _tenure = 3;
  double _emi = 0, _totalInterest = 0, _totalPayable = 0;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _calculate();
  }

  void _calculate() {
    // Personal loans usually calculated in years for UI, but logic uses months
    double months = _tenure * 12;
    double emi = LoanCalculatorHelpers.calculateEMI(_amount, _rate, months);

    setState(() {
      _emi = emi;
      _totalPayable = emi * months;
      _totalInterest = _totalPayable - _amount;
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: PersonalLoanColors.background,
      body: Column(
        children: [
          PersonalLoanAppBar(
            onBack: () => Navigator.pop(context),
            onBookmark: () => ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(const SnackBar(content: Text("Added to bookmarks"))),
          ),
          Expanded(
            child: SingleChildScrollView(
              child: Column(
                children: [
                  const SizedBox(height: 16),
                  PersonalLoanResultCard(emi: _emi, totalInterest: _totalInterest, totalPayable: _totalPayable),
                  PersonalLoanInputCard(
                    amount: _amount, rate: _rate, tenure: _tenure,
                    onAmount: (v) { setState(() => _amount = v); _calculate(); },
                    onRate: (v) { setState(() => _rate = v); _calculate(); },
                    onTenure: (v) { setState(() => _tenure = v); _calculate(); },
                  ),
                  PersonalLoanBreakdownCard(principal: _amount, interest: _totalInterest),
                ],
              ),
            ),
          ),
          PersonalLoanBottomBar(
            onAmortization: () => ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(const SnackBar(content: Text("Amortization Coming Soon"))),
            onSave: () => ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text("Quote Saved: â‚¹${_emi.round()}"))),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 39: saved_history_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\saved_history_screen.dart`
**Size:** 3.73 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../services/saved_calculation_service.dart';
import '../models/saved_calculation_model.dart';
import '../widgets/history/saved_calculation_card.dart';
import '../widgets/history/history_app_bar.dart';
import '../widgets/history/history_empty_state.dart';
import '../widgets/history/history_filter_sheet.dart';
import '../utils/app_colors.dart';
import 'home_dashboard_screen.dart';

class SavedHistoryScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const SavedHistoryScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<SavedHistoryScreen> createState() => _SavedHistoryScreenState();
}

class _SavedHistoryScreenState extends State<SavedHistoryScreen> {
  final SavedCalculationService _service = SavedCalculationService();
  List<SavedCalculationModel> _allCalculations = [];
  List<SavedCalculationModel> _filteredCalculations = [];
  bool _isLoading = true;
  String _selectedFilter = 'All';
  String _selectedSort = 'Newest First';

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _loadData();
  }

  Future<void> _loadData() async {
    setState(() => _isLoading = true);
    final data = await _service.getAllCalculations();
    setState(() {
      _allCalculations = data;
      _applyFilters();
      _isLoading = false;
    });
  }

  void _applyFilters() {
    _filteredCalculations = _allCalculations.where((calc) {
      if (_selectedFilter == 'All') return true;
      return calc.type == _selectedFilter;
    }).toList();

    _applySorting();
  }

  void _applySorting() {
    if (_selectedSort == 'Newest First') {
      _filteredCalculations.sort((a, b) => b.date.compareTo(a.date));
    } else if (_selectedSort == 'Oldest First') {
      _filteredCalculations.sort((a, b) => a.date.compareTo(b.date));
    } else if (_selectedSort == 'Amount: High to Low') {
      _filteredCalculations.sort((a, b) => b.principalAmount.compareTo(a.principalAmount));
    } else if (_selectedSort == 'Amount: Low to High') {
      _filteredCalculations.sort((a, b) => a.principalAmount.compareTo(b.principalAmount));
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundLight,
      appBar: HistoryAppBar(
        onFilterTap: () => _showFilterSheet(),
        onBackTap: () => Navigator.pushReplacement(
          context,
          MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const HomeDashboardScreen()),
        ),
      ),
      body: _isLoading
          ? const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator())
          : _filteredCalculations.isEmpty
          ? HistoryEmptyState(onAddNew: () => Navigator.pop(context))
          : ListView.builder(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
        itemCount: _filteredCalculations.length,
        itemBuilder: (context, index) {
          return SavedCalculationCard(
            data: _filteredCalculations[index],
            onDelete: () => _deleteItem(_filteredCalculations[index].id),
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showFilterSheet() async {
    final result = await showModalBottomSheet<Map<String, String>>(
      context: context,
      builder: (_) => HistoryFilterSheet(
        selectedFilter: _selectedFilter,
        selectedSort: _selectedSort,
      ),
    );
    if (result != null) {
      setState(() {
        _selectedFilter = result['filter']!;
        _selectedSort = result['sort']!;
        _applyFilters();
      });
    }
  }

  Future<void> _deleteItem(String id) async {
    await _service.deleteCalculation(id);
    _loadData();
    if (mounted) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        const SnackBar(content: Text('Calculation deleted successfully')),
      );
    }
  }
}

```

### File 40: signup_screen.dart

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../utils/app_colors.dart';
import '../widgets/signup/signup_header.dart';
import '../widgets/signup/signup_form.dart';
import '../widgets/signup/signup_validator.dart';

class SignupScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const SignupScreen({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  State<SignupScreen> createState() => _SignupScreenState();
}

class _SignupScreenState extends State<SignupScreen> {
  final _nameController = TextEditingController();
  final _emailController = TextEditingController();
  final _phoneController = TextEditingController();
  final _passwordController = TextEditingController();
  final _confirmPasswordController = TextEditingController();
  bool _agreedToTerms = false;

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _nameController.dispose();
    _emailController.dispose();
    _phoneController.dispose();
    _passwordController.dispose();
    _confirmPasswordController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  void _handleSignup() async {
    final validator = SignupValidator(context);

    final result = await validator.validateAndSave(
      name: _nameController.text,
      email: _emailController.text,
      phone: _phoneController.text,
      password: _passwordController.text,
      confirmPassword: _confirmPasswordController.text,
      agreedToTerms: _agreedToTerms,
    );

    if (result) {
      // Validation successful, navigation handled in validator
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(
        decoration: BoxDecoration(gradient: AppColors.primaryGradient),
        child: SafeArea(
          child: Column(
            children: [
              SignupHeader(onBack: () => Navigator.pop(context)),
              Expanded(
                child: Container(
                  decoration: const BoxDecoration(
                    color: Colors.white,
                    borderRadius: BorderRadius.vertical(top: Radius.circular(24)),
                  ),
                  child: SingleChildScrollView(
                    padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
                    child: SignupForm(
                      nameController: _nameController,
                      emailController: _emailController,
                      phoneController: _phoneController,
                      passwordController: _passwordController,
                      confirmPasswordController: _confirmPasswordController,
                      agreedToTerms: _agreedToTerms,
                      onTermsChanged: (value) {
                        setState(() => _agreedToTerms = value);
                      },
                      onSignup: _handleSignup,
                      onLoginTap: () => Navigator.pop(context),
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../utils/app_colors.dart';
import 'login_screen.dart';

class SplashScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const SplashScreen({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  State<SplashScreen> createState() => _SplashScreenState();
}

class _SplashScreenState extends State<SplashScreen> {
  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _navigateToLogin();
  }

  _navigateToLogin() async {
    await Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 3));
    if (mounted) {
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const LoginScreen()),
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(
        decoration: BoxDecoration(gradient: AppColors.primaryGradient),
        child: Stack(
          children: [
            _buildDecorativeCircles(),
            Center(
              child: Column(
                mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                children: [
                  _buildAppIcon(),
                  const SizedBox(height: 24),
                  _buildAppTitle(),
                  const SizedBox(height: 8),
                  _buildTagline(),
                ],
              ),
            ),
            _buildLoadingIndicator(),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildAppIcon() {
    return Container(
      height: 96,
      width: 96,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.1),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
        border: Border.all(color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.2)),
      ),
      child: const Icon(Icons.calculate, size: 56, color: Colors.white),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildAppTitle() {
    return const Text(
      'EMI Pro',
      style: TextStyle(
        fontSize: 42,
        fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
        color: Colors.white,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildTagline() {
    return Text(
      'Calculate Your Loans Smartly',
      style: TextStyle(
        fontSize: 18,
        color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.8),
        fontWeight: FontWeight.w500,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildDecorativeCircles() {
    return Stack(
      children: [
        Positioned(
          top: -100,
          left: -100,
          child: Container(
            height: 250,
            width: 250,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              shape: BoxShape.circle,
              color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.05),
            ),
          ),
        ),
        Positioned(
          bottom: -130,
          right: -130,
          child: Container(
            height: 320,
            width: 320,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              shape: BoxShape.circle,
              color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.1),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildLoadingIndicator() {
    return Positioned(
      bottom: 64,
      left: 0,
      right: 0,
      child: Column(
        children: [
          Row(
            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
            children: List.generate(
              3,
                  (index) => Container(
                margin: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 3),
                height: 6,
                width: 6,
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  shape: BoxShape.circle,
                  color: index == 0
                      ? Colors.white
                      : Colors.white.withOpacity(0.4),
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
```

### File 42: home_dashboard_data.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\home_dashboard_data.dart`
**Size:** 1.39 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';

class HomeDashboardData {
  String userName = 'User';
  final ValueNotifier<bool> isLoading = ValueNotifier(true);
  final ValueNotifier<int> savedCalculationsCount = ValueNotifier(0);
  final ValueNotifier<List<Map<String, dynamic>>> recentCalculations = ValueNotifier([]);

  Future<void> loadUserData() async {
    isLoading.value = true;

    try {
      final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();

      userName = prefs.getString('user_name') ?? 'Prahlad Das';

      final calculationKeys = prefs.getKeys()
          .where((key) => key.startsWith('calculation_'))
          .toList();

      savedCalculationsCount.value = calculationKeys.length;

      final recentCalcs = <Map<String, dynamic>>[];
      for (var key in calculationKeys.take(5)) {
        final calcData = prefs.getString(key);
        if (calcData != null) {
          final parts = calcData.split('|');
          if (parts.length == 3) {
            recentCalcs.add({
              'amount': parts[0],
              'type': parts[1],
              'date': parts[2],
            });
          }
        }
      }

      recentCalculations.value = recentCalcs;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('Error loading user data: $e');
    } finally {
      isLoading.value = false;
    }
  }
}

```

### File 43: loan_calculator_helpers.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\loan_calculator_helpers.dart`
**Size:** 1.64 KB

```dart
import 'dart:math';
import 'package:intl/intl.dart';

class LoanCalculatorHelpers {
  // 1. Calculate EMI
  static double calculateEMI(double principal, double annualRate, double tenureInMonths) {
    if (principal <= 0 || tenureInMonths <= 0) return 0;

    double monthlyRate = annualRate / 12 / 100;

    if (monthlyRate == 0) {
      return principal / tenureInMonths;
    }

    double emi = (principal * monthlyRate * pow(1 + monthlyRate, tenureInMonths)) /
        (pow(1 + monthlyRate, tenureInMonths) - 1);

    return emi;
  }

  // 2. Format with Commas (e.g., 10,000)
  static String formatWithCommas(double amount) {
    final formatter = NumberFormat.decimalPattern('en_IN');
    return formatter.format(amount.round());
  }

  // 3. Short Currency Format for Sliders (e.g., 1L, 50k)
  static String formatCurrency(double amount) {
    if (amount >= 10000000) {
      return '${(amount / 10000000).toStringAsFixed(1)}Cr';
    } else if (amount >= 100000) {
      return '${(amount / 100000).toStringAsFixed(1)}L';
    } else if (amount >= 1000) {
      return '${(amount / 1000).toStringAsFixed(0)}k';
    } else {
      return amount.toStringAsFixed(0);
    }
  }

  // 4. Amount to Words (FIXED: This was missing)
  static String amountToWords(double amount) {
    if (amount >= 10000000) {
      return '${(amount / 10000000).toStringAsFixed(2)} Crores';
    } else if (amount >= 100000) {
      return '${(amount / 100000).toStringAsFixed(2)} Lakhs';
    } else if (amount >= 1000) {
      return '${(amount / 1000).toStringAsFixed(2)} Thousand';
    } else {
      return amount.toStringAsFixed(0);
    }
  }
}
```

### File 44: saved_calculation_service.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\saved_calculation_service.dart`
**Size:** 1.15 KB

```dart
import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';
import '../models/saved_calculation_model.dart';

class SavedCalculationService {
  static const String _storageKeyPrefix = 'calc_data_';

  Future<void> saveCalculation(SavedCalculationModel calculation) async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.setString(
        '$_storageKeyPrefix${calculation.id}',
        calculation.toJson()
    );
  }

  Future<List<SavedCalculationModel>> getAllCalculations() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    final keys = prefs.getKeys().where((k) => k.startsWith(_storageKeyPrefix));

    List<SavedCalculationModel> list = [];
    for (String key in keys) {
      final jsonStr = prefs.getString(key);
      if (jsonStr != null) {
        list.add(SavedCalculationModel.fromJson(jsonStr));
      }
    }
    // Sort by date (newest first)
    list.sort((a, b) => b.date.compareTo(a.date));
    return list;
  }

  Future<void> deleteCalculation(String id) async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    await prefs.remove('$_storageKeyPrefix$id');
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../utils/app_colors.dart';

class CustomTextField extends StatefulWidget {
  final String label;
  final String placeholder;
  final IconData icon;
  final TextInputType keyboardType;
  final bool isPassword;
  final TextEditingController? controller;

  const CustomTextField({
    Key? key,
    required this.label,
    required this.placeholder,
    required this.icon,
    this.keyboardType = TextInputType.text,
    this.isPassword = false,
    this.controller,
  }) : super(key: key);

  @override
  State<CustomTextField> createState() => _CustomTextFieldState();
}

class _CustomTextFieldState extends State<CustomTextField> {
  bool _obscureText = true;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
      children: [
        Text(
          widget.label,
          style: const TextStyle(
            fontSize: 14,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.w500,
            color: AppColors.textDark,
          ),
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 8),
        Container(
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: Colors.grey[50],
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
            border: Border.all(color: AppColors.borderColor),
          ),
          child: Row(
            children: [
              Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.only(left: 16, right: 8),
                child: Icon(widget.icon, color: AppColors.textLight, size: 20),
              ),
              Expanded(
                child: TextField(
                  controller: widget.controller,
                  keyboardType: widget.keyboardType,
                  obscureText: widget.isPassword ? _obscureText : false,
                  decoration: InputDecoration(
                    hintText: widget.placeholder,
                    hintStyle: const TextStyle(color: AppColors.textLight),
                    border: InputBorder.none,
                    contentPadding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
                  ),
                ),
              ),
              if (widget.isPassword)
                IconButton(
                  icon: Icon(
                    _obscureText ? Icons.visibility : Icons.visibility_off,
                    color: AppColors.textLight,
                  ),
                  onPressed: () {
                    setState(() {
                      _obscureText = !_obscureText;
                    });
                  },
                ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
class LoanCalculatorBottomActions extends StatelessWidget {

                  children: [
                    Icon(Icons.analytics, size: 20),
                    SizedBox(width: 8),
                    Text(
                      'View Detailed Amortization',
                      style: TextStyle(
                        fontSize: 15,
                        fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                      ),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 10),
            SizedBox(
              width: double.infinity,
              child: OutlinedButton(
                onPressed: () => _saveCalculation(context),
                style: OutlinedButton.styleFrom(
                  side: const BorderSide(color: AppColors.primaryBlue, width: 2),
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 14),
                  shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
                    borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
                  ),
                ),
                child: const Row(
                  mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                  children: [
                    Icon(Icons.save, size: 20, color: AppColors.primaryBlue),
                    SizedBox(width: 8),
                    Text(
                      'Save Calculation',
                      style: TextStyle(
                        fontSize: 15,
                        fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                        color: AppColors.primaryBlue,
                      ),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  // PRODUCTION-READY: Clean Save Logic
  Future<void> _saveCalculation(BuildContext context) async {
    try {
      // FIXED: Convert months to years properly and ROUND to whole number
      double tenureInYears;
      if (isYears) {
        tenureInYears = tenure.roundToDouble(); // Already in years, just round
      } else {
        tenureInYears = (tenure / 12).roundToDouble(); // Convert months to years
      }

      final calculation = SavedCalculationModel(
        id: DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch.toString(),
        type: 'Home Loan',
        principalAmount: loanAmount,
        interestRate: interestRate,
        tenure: tenureInYears, // Always save clean whole years
        monthlyEMI: monthlyEMI,
        date: DateTime.now(),
      );

      final service = SavedCalculationService();
      await service.saveCalculation(calculation);

      if (context.mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(
            content: Text('Calculation saved successfully!'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.green,
            duration: Duration(seconds: 2),
          ),
        );

        // Auto navigate after success
        await Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 1));

        if (context.mounted) {
          Navigator.pushReplacement(
            context,
            MaterialPageRoute(
              builder: (context) => const SavedHistoryScreen(),
            ),
          );
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      if (context.mounted) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(
            content: Text('Error saving: $e'),
            backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          ),
        );
      }
    }
  }

  void _showAmortizationSheet(BuildContext context) {
    showModalBottomSheet(
      context: context,
      isScrollControlled: true,
      backgroundColor: Colors.transparent,
      barrierColor: Colors.black54,
      builder: (BuildContext context) {
        return DraggableScrollableSheet(
          initialChildSize: 0.9,
          minChildSize: 0.5,
          maxChildSize: 0.95,
          expand: false,
          builder: (context, scrollController) {
            return Material(
              color: Colors.white,
              borderRadius: const BorderRadius.vertical(top: Radius.circular(20)),
              clipBehavior: Clip.antiAlias,
              child: Column(
                children: [
                  Container(
                    margin: const EdgeInsets.only(top: 12, bottom: 8),
                    width: 40,
                    height: 4,
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(
                      color: Colors.grey[300],
                      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(2),
                    ),
                  ),
                  Container(
                    padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 12),
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(
                      color: Colors.white,
                      border: Border(bottom: BorderSide(color: Colors.grey[200]!)),
                    ),
                    child: Row(
                      children: [
                        Container(
                          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(8),
                          decoration: BoxDecoration(
                            color: AppColors.primaryBlue.withOpacity(0.1),
                            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
                          ),
                          child: const Icon(Icons.analytics, color: AppColors.primaryBlue, size: 24),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        const Expanded(
                          child: Text(
                            'Amortization Schedule',
                            style: TextStyle(fontSize: 18, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: Colors.black87),
                          ),
                        ),
                        IconButton(
                          icon: const Icon(Icons.close, color: Colors.black54),
                          onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
                          padding: EdgeInsets.zero,
                          constraints: const BoxConstraints(),
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ),
                  Expanded(
                    child: ListView(
                      controller: scrollController,
                      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
                      children: [
                        _buildSummaryCard(),
                        const SizedBox(height: 24),
                        const Text('Year-wise Breakdown', style: TextStyle(fontSize: 16, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: Colors.black87)),
                        const SizedBox(height: 12),
                        ..._buildAmortizationList(),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            );
          },
        );
      },
    );
  }

  Widget _buildSummaryCard() {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        gradient: const LinearGradient(
          colors: [AppColors.primaryBlue, AppColors.accentPurple],
          begin: Alignment.topLeft,
          end: Alignment.bottomRight,
        ),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
        boxShadow: [BoxShadow(color: AppColors.primaryBlue.withOpacity(0.3), blurRadius: 12, offset: const Offset(0, 4))],
      ),
      child: Column(
        children: [
          _buildSummaryRow('Loan Amount', LoanCalculatorHelpers.formatCurrency(loanAmount)),
          const Padding(padding: EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 12), child: Divider(color: Colors.white24, thickness: 1)),
          _buildSummaryRow('Monthly EMI', 'â‚¹${monthlyEMI.toStringAsFixed(0)}'),
          const Padding(padding: EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 12), child: Divider(color: Colors.white24, thickness: 1)),
          _buildSummaryRow('Total Interest', LoanCalculatorHelpers.formatCurrency(totalInterest)),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildSummaryRow(String label, String value) {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
      children: [
        Text(label, style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white, fontSize: 14, fontWeight: FontWeight.w500)),
        Text(value, style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white, fontSize: 18, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold)),
      ],
    );
  }

  List<Widget> _buildAmortizationList() {
    final years = isYears ? tenure.toInt() : (tenure / 12).ceil();
    final list = <Widget>[];
    double remainingPrincipal = loanAmount;

    for (int year = 1; year <= years; year++) {
      final monthsInYear = (year == years && (tenureInMonths % 12) != 0) ? (tenureInMonths % 12).toInt() : 12;
      final yearlyPayment = monthlyEMI * monthsInYear;
      final yearlyInterestRate = interestRate / 100;
      final interestForYear = remainingPrincipal * yearlyInterestRate;
      final principalForYear = yearlyPayment - interestForYear;
      remainingPrincipal = (remainingPrincipal - principalForYear).clamp(0.0, double.infinity);

      list.add(
        Container(
          margin: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 12),
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: Colors.white,
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
            border: Border.all(color: Colors.grey[300]!),
            boxShadow: [BoxShadow(color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.05), blurRadius: 8, offset: const Offset(0, 2))],
          ),
          child: Column(
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
            children: [
              Row(
                mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
                children: [
                  Container(
                    padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12, vertical: 6),
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(color: AppColors.primaryBlue.withOpacity(0.1), borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(6)),
                    child: Text('Year $year', style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 14, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: AppColors.primaryBlue)),
                  ),
                  Text(LoanCalculatorHelpers.formatCurrency(yearlyPayment), style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 16, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, color: Colors.black87)),
                ],
              ),
              const SizedBox(height: 12),
              Container(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
                decoration: BoxDecoration(color: Colors.grey[50], borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8)),
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    Row(
                      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
                      children: [
                        Row(children: [Icon(Icons.account_balance_wallet, size: 16, color: Colors.green[700]), const SizedBox(width: 6), Text('Principal', style: TextStyle(fontSize: 13, color: Colors.grey[600]))]),
                        Text(LoanCalculatorHelpers.formatCurrency(principalForYear), style: TextStyle(fontSize: 14, fontWeight: FontWeight.w600, color: Colors.green[700])),
                      ],
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(height: 8),
                    Row(
                      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
                      children: [
                        Row(children: [Icon(Icons.percent, size: 16, color: Colors.orange[700]), const SizedBox(width: 6), Text('Interest', style: TextStyle(fontSize: 13, color: Colors.grey[600]))]),
                        Text(LoanCalculatorHelpers.formatCurrency(interestForYear), style: TextStyle(fontSize: 14, fontWeight: FontWeight.w600, color: Colors.orange[700])),
                      ],
                    ),
                    const Padding(padding: EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 8), child: Divider(thickness: 1, height: 1)),
                    Row(
                      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
                      children: [
                        Row(children: [Icon(Icons.money_off, size: 16, color: Colors.blue[700]), const SizedBox(width: 6), Text('Balance', style: TextStyle(fontSize: 13, color: Colors.grey[600]))]),
                        Text(LoanCalculatorHelpers.formatCurrency(remainingPrincipal), style: TextStyle(fontSize: 14, fontWeight: FontWeight.w600, color: Colors.blue[700])),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      );
    }
    return list;
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class LoanCalculatorBreakdown extends StatelessWidget {

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {

          ),
          Container(
            width: 1,
            height: 60,
            color: Colors.grey[200],
          ),

              Icons.percent,
              'INTEREST',
              LoanCalculatorHelpers.formatCurrency(totalInterest),
              Colors.orange,
            ),
          ),
          Container(
            width: 1,
            height: 60,
            color: Colors.grey[200],
          ),
          Expanded(
            child: _buildBreakdownItem(
              Icons.account_balance_wallet,
              'TOTAL',
              LoanCalculatorHelpers.formatCurrency(totalAmount),
              AppColors.accentPurple,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBreakdownItem(IconData icon, String label, String value, Color color) {
    return Column(
      children: [
        Container(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(10),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: color.withValues(alpha: 0.1),
            shape: BoxShape.circle,
          ),
          child: Icon(icon, color: color, size: 20),
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 8),
        Text(
          label,
          style: TextStyle(
            fontSize: 9,
            color: Colors.grey[600],
            fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
          ),
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 4),
        Text(
          value,
          style: const TextStyle(
            fontSize: 13,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}
```
